doWithAds = function(inside, failureMessage){

'generic' in window &&
'ad_utils' in window &&
'custom' in window &&

ueLogError(e);
}

(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined') ){
console.error(failureMessage);
}
}
} else {

(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined') ){
console.error(failureMessage);
}
}
};
